title	"Boss"
pageid	29375
text	
*	`<div class="mw-parser-output"><div class="noexcerpt noprint nomobile navigation-not-searchable rs-external-header-links" style="display:none"><span class="rs-header-icon rs-header-icon-rs" data-interwiki="rsw" data-page="Boss" data-wikiname="The RuneScape Wiki">Boss</span></div>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">This article is about the <a href="/w/Strongest" class="mw-redirect" title="Strongest">strongest</a> class of monsters. For other uses, see <a href="/w/Boss_(disambiguation)" title="Boss (disambiguation)">Boss (disambiguation)</a>.</div>\n<figure class="mw-halign-right" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/w/File:Boss.png" class="mw-file-description"><img src="/images/thumb/Boss.png/150px-Boss.png?fb192" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="150" height="145" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/images/thumb/Boss.png/300px-Boss.png?fb192 2x" data-file-width="1382" data-file-height="1333" /></a><figcaption></figcaption></figure>\n<p>A <b>boss</b> is a powerful, usually unique <a href="/w/Monster" title="Monster">monster</a> that is fought to accomplish an objective, be it the advancement or completion of a <a href="/w/Quest" class="mw-redirect" title="Quest">quest</a> or <a href="/w/Minigame" class="mw-redirect" title="Minigame">minigame</a>, or as part of a team <a href="/w/Player-versus-monster" class="mw-redirect" title="Player-versus-monster">player-versus-monster</a> event. Many quests feature boss fights at their climaxes; such bosses are often the main antagonists of the quests or quest series, or are somehow related to the main antagonist(s). Some monsters that are commonly referred to as bosses are very powerful monsters that reside in <a href="/w/Multi-combat_area" class="mw-redirect" title="Multi-combat area">multi-combat areas</a>; these monsters are commonly fought by teams of players in search of highly valuable <a href="/w/Drops" title="Drops">drops</a>. Many bosses have extremely high <a href="/w/Combat_level" title="Combat level">combat levels</a>, and most of the <a href="/w/Strongest_monsters" class="mw-redirect" title="Strongest monsters">strongest monsters</a> in the game are bosses. With the exception of <a href="/w/Bryophyta" title="Bryophyta">Bryophyta</a> and <a href="/w/Obor" title="Obor">Obor</a>, bosses are exclusive to <a href="/w/Members" title="Members">members</a>.\n</p><p><a href="/w/Dwarf_multicannons" class="mw-redirect" title="Dwarf multicannons">Dwarf multicannons</a> often cannot be set up in the areas of many bosses, and many are immune or resistant to other effects, such as <a href="/w/Freeze" class="mw-redirect" title="Freeze">freeze</a> and <a href="/w/Poison" title="Poison">poison</a>. Others may have different restrictions; for example, <a href="/w/Prayer" title="Prayer">Prayer</a> cannot be used during the fights with the final bosses of <a href="/w/Recipe_for_Disaster" title="Recipe for Disaster">Recipe for Disaster</a>. Most bosses (e.g. bosses like the <a href="/w/Corporeal_Beast" title="Corporeal Beast">Corporeal Beast</a>) also reside in a multi-way area; very few reside in <a href="/w/Single-way" class="mw-redirect" title="Single-way">single-way</a> areas or instances.\n</p><p>Excluding minigame and quest bosses, each boss has its own <a href="/w/HiScores" title="HiScores">hiscore table</a>, tracking the players with the most kills, or raid completions in the case of raid bosses. Each of these bosses (or raids) also has its own set of <a href="/w/Combat_achievements" class="mw-redirect" title="Combat achievements">combat achievements</a> and, with the exception of the <a href="/w/Deranged_archaeologist" title="Deranged archaeologist">Deranged archaeologist</a>, each one also has unique drops in the <a href="/w/Collection_log" title="Collection log">collection log</a>. Most bosses will generate a message upon kill telling the player what drop(s) they have obtained. For example, if players are at <a href="/w/General_Graardor" title="General Graardor">General Graardor</a> and kill him (and drops <a href="/w/Bandos_tassets" title="Bandos tassets">Bandos tassets</a>), a message will appear in the game box saying "Player name received item: Bandos tassets".\n</p>\n<div id="toc" class="toc" role="navigation" aria-labelledby="mw-toc-heading"><input type="checkbox" role="button" id="toctogglecheckbox" class="toctogglecheckbox" style="display:none" /><div class="toctitle" lang="en-GB" dir="ltr"><h2 id="mw-toc-heading">Contents</h2><span <span class="toctext">See also</span></a></li>\n</ul>\n</div>\n\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="List_of_bosses">List of bosses</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/Boss?section=1&amp;veaction=edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: List of bosses">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Boss?action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section&#039;s source code: List of bosses">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="World_bosses">World bosses</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/Boss?section=2&amp;veaction=edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: World bosses">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Boss?action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section&#039;s source code: World bosses">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>World bosses spawn across <a href="/w/Gielinor" title="Gielinor">Gielinor</a> either out in the open or in their lairs. World bosses are defined as bosses which spawn naturally, on their own, and can be killed at any time, as opposed to instanced bosses which spawn only in private lairs based on the actions of the player to whom the instance belongs. Some world bosses may, however, be killed in private instances for a price. Some world bosses, namely the <a href="/w/Barrows_brothers" title="Barrows brothers">Barrows brothers</a> and <a href="/w/God_Wars_Dungeon" title="God Wars Dungeon">God Wars Dungeon</a> generals, also have additional requirements and mechanics related to finding and killing them. In the case of the Barrows brothers, they do not drop <a href="/w/Loot" class="mw-redirect" title="Loot">loot</a> directly, but their defeat instead contributes to a single <a href="/w/Chest_(Barrows)" title="Chest (Barrows)">reward</a>.\n</p>\n<table class="wikitable sortable mw-collapsible">\n<tbody><tr>\n<th class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Wilderness bosses">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Boss?action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section&#039;s source code: Wilderness bosses">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>\n<p>The following world bosses are specifically located within the <a href="/w/Wilderness" title="Wilderness">Wilderness</a>, where players may attack each other. The one exception is the King Black Dragon: his lair where the fight takes place is not located in the Wilderness, but it can only be accessed through Wilderness, and is thus still considered risky.\n</p>\n<table class="wikitable sortable mw-collapsible">\n<tbody><tr>\n<th colspan="2">Boss\n</th>\n<th>Level\n</th>\n<th>Hitpoints\n</th>\n<th>Attack id="Instanced_bosses">Instanced bosses</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/Boss?section=4&amp;veaction=edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Instanced bosses">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Boss?action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section&#039;s source code: Instanced bosses">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>As opposed to world bosses, instanced bosses are fought in their own arena. They are generally fought alone, with the exception of <a href="/w/The_Nightmare" title="The Nightmare">The Nightmare</a>, which is a group instanced boss, and the <a href="/w/Royal_Titans" title="Royal Titans">Royal Titans</a> alongside <a href="/w/Yama" title="Yama">Yama</a>, which are a duo instanced boss. Spawning instanced bosses either requires an action (<a href="/w/Zulrah" title="Zulrah">Zulrah</a> and <a href="/w/Vorkath" title="Vorkath">Vorkath</a>), while others simply spawn upon entering the instance (<a href="/w/Amoxliatl" title="Amoxliatl">Amoxliatl</a>, <a href="/w/Royal_Titans" title="Royal Titans">Royal Titans</a>, <a href="/w/Phantom_Muspah" title="Phantom Muspah">Phantom Muspah</a> and both forms of the Nightmare).\n</p>\n<table class="wikitable sortable mw-collapsible">\n<tbody><tr>\n<th colspan="2">Boss\n</th>\n<th>Level\n</th>\n<th>Hitpoints\n</th>\n<th>Attack href="/w/Boss?section=5&amp;veaction=edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: The Forgotten Four">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Boss?action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section&#039;s source code: The Forgotten Four">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>\n<p>The following bosses can be fought during and after completing <a href="/w/Desert_Treasure_II_-_The_Fallen_Empire" title="Desert Treasure II - The Fallen Empire">Desert Treasure II - The Fallen Empire</a>. The versions fought after completing the quest have increased stats, dealing more damage with their auto-attacks and mechanics, but are otherwise the same as the quest variants. An even stronger variant, known as awakened, can be fought with the use of an <a href="/w/Awakener%27s_orb" title="Awakener&#39;s orb">awakener's orb</a>. These awakened variants have an even larger stat increase, their base mechanics are enhanced and with the exception of the Whisperer, gain new mechanics.\n</p><p>In normal mode, if the player has less than five kills on the boss and die, they will only pay 20% of the total fee.\n</p>\n<table class="wikitable sortable mw-collapsible">\n<tbody><tr>\n<th class="mw-headline" id="Sporadic_bosses">Sporadic bosses</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/Boss?section=6&amp;veaction=edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Sporadic bosses">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Boss?action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section&#039;s source code: Sporadic bosses">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>\n<p>Sporadic bosses are those that cannot be fought whenever the player wishes. Instead, they require a special item of some sort to gain access to them, which is obtained by partaking in other more common activities. Naturally, these bosses will also be instanced given the nature of their sporadic logistic. Of this list, Obor and Bryophyta are notably the only <a href="/w/Free-to-play" title="Free-to-play">free-to-play</a> bosses outside of quests.\n</p>\n<table class="wikitable sortable mw-collapsible">\n<tbody><tr>\n<th colspan="2">Boss\n</th>\n<th>Level\n</th>\n<th>Hitpoints\n</th>\n<th>Attack style(s)\n</th>\n<th>Location\n</th>\n<th>Requirements\n</th>\n<th>Collection grow</span>\n</li>\n</ol></div></div>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Slayer_bosses">Slayer bosses</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/Boss?section=7&amp;veaction=edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Slayer bosses">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Boss?action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section&#039;s source code: Slayer bosses">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Slayer bosses are a specific set of bosses that are only unlocked by training <a href="/w/Slayer" title="Slayer">Slayer</a>. Each one corresponds to another monster commonly assigned for Slayer tasks, which, with the exception of <a href="/w/Hellhound" title="Hellhound">hellhounds</a>, are also unlocked by training Slayer. In addition to a Slayer level requirement, each boss requires a task for either the boss itself or the equivalent monster in order to be fought.\n</p>\n<table class="wikitable sortable class="mw-headline" id="Minigame_bosses">Minigame bosses</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/Boss?section=8&amp;veaction=edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Minigame bosses">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Boss?action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section&#039;s source code: Minigame bosses">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>These bosses are fought as parts of instanced <a href="/w/Minigames" title="Minigames">minigames</a>. The combat achievements for these minigames usually (but not always) relate to or at least require the defeat of the bosses, and, like other boss <a href="/w/Pet" title="Pet">pets</a>, pets rewarded by these minigames are typically smaller versions of the bosses.\n</p>\n<table class="wikitable sortable mw-collapsible">\n<tbody><tr>\n<th id="Skilling_bosses">Skilling bosses</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/Boss?section=9&amp;veaction=edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Skilling bosses">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Boss?action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section&#039;s source code: Skilling bosses">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Skilling bosses are world bosses that are not fought conventionally, but rather by utilising non-combat skills to defeat them, either directly or indirectly. For this reason, they can be very different experiences to more conventional bosses, and require entirely different gear and equipment. The <a href="/w/Hespori" title="Hespori">Hespori</a> also is strongly linked to a skill (requiring <a href="/w/Farming" title="Farming">Farming</a> to spawn and giving Farming XP), but the fight against it only uses normal combat.\n</p>\n<table class="wikitable sortable mw-collapsible">\n<tbody><tr>\n<th colspan="2">Boss\n</th>\n<th>Skills used\n</th>\n<th>Combat data-file-height="22" /></a></span></span><a href="/w/Uncut_onyx" title="Uncut onyx">Uncut onyx</a>\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Raids">Raids</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/Boss?section=10&amp;veaction=edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Raids">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Boss?action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section&#039;s source code: Raids">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p><a href="/w/Raids" title="Raids">Raids</a> are high-level activities with a set of bosses that players can fight either alone or with a team.\n</p>\n<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Chambers_of_Xeric">Chambers of Xeric</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/Boss?section=11&amp;veaction=edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Chambers of Xeric">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Boss?action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section&#039;s source code: Chambers of Xeric">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>\n<p>Bosses within the <a href="/w/Chambers_of_Xeric" title="Chambers of Xeric">Chambers of Xeric</a> are sporadic: as the layout of each raid is randomised, the bosses that players will encounter as well as their order may vary, with the exception of the <a href="/w/Great_Olm" title="Great Olm">Great Olm</a>, which appears at the end of every raid. This is not the case if the <a href="/w/Chambers_of_Xeric/Challenge_Mode" title="Chambers of Xeric/Challenge Mode">Challenge Mode</a> is enabled, where each boss is encountered and there is no randomisation. Each boss' stats also scale to the amount of players in the raid and their combat level. All bosses except ice demon and the Great Olm drop potions, seeds or ingredients to use in the raid; once the Great Olm is defeated, the exit is opened and players can collect their loot, the quality of which scales to their performance in the raid.\n</p>\n<table class="wikitable sortable mw-collapsible">\n<tbody><tr>\n<th colspan="2">Boss\n</th>\n<th>Attack style(s)\n</th>\n<th>Special attacks or Olm">multitude of special attacks</a>\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Theatre_of_Blood">Theatre of Blood</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/Boss?section=12&amp;veaction=edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Theatre of Blood">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Boss?action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section&#039;s source code: Theatre of Blood">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>\n<p>Unlike the <a href="/w/Chambers_of_Xeric" title="Chambers of Xeric">Chambers of Xeric</a>, bosses within the <a href="/w/Theatre_of_Blood" title="Theatre of Blood">Theatre of Blood</a> take place in a predetermined order. Their hitpoints are scaled depending on the number of players from three to five; if there are only one or two players, the scaling for three players is used, and five is the maximum number of players per team. Bosses do not drop anything, although there are resource chests where players can obtain potions and food for upcoming encounters; after defeating <a href="/w/Verzik_Vitur" title="Verzik Vitur">Verzik Vitur</a>, the entrance to her vault is opened where players can obtain their loot, the quality of which scales to their performance in the raid.\n</p>\n<table class="wikitable sortable class="mw-headline" id="Tombs_of_Amascut">Tombs of Amascut</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/Boss?section=13&amp;veaction=edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Tombs of Amascut">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Boss?action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section&#039;s source code: Tombs of Amascut">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>\n<p>In the <a href="/w/Tombs_of_Amascut" title="Tombs of Amascut">Tombs of Amascut</a>, players are able to face each of the first four bosses, namely, Akkha, Ba-Ba, Kephri, and Zebak in any order they choose. After the player has defeated all 4, they may challenge the wardens as the final boss. Tombs of Amascut is unique in that it has <a href="/w/Invocations" class="mw-redirect" title="Invocations">invocations</a>, which is a system that allows the individual to increase the difficulty of the bosses in a modular fashion. As such, the numbers provided for level and hitpoints are based on a raid with <i><b>No Invocations.</b></i> The strength of the bosses will scale with each additional invocation added to each boss.\n</p>\n<table class="wikitable sortable mw-collapsible">\n<tbody><tr>\n<th colspan="2">Boss\n</th>\n<th>Level\n</th>\n<th>Hitpoints\n</th>\n<th>Attack class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/Boss?section=14&amp;veaction=edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Quest bosses">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Boss?action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section&#039;s source code: Quest bosses">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<figure class="mw-halign-right" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/w/File:Culinaromancer.png" class="mw-file-description"><img src="/images/thumb/Culinaromancer.png/150px-Culinaromancer.png?1076b" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="150" height="406" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/images/thumb/Culinaromancer.png/300px-Culinaromancer.png?1076b 2x" data-file-width="363" data-file-height="982" /></a><figcaption>The <a href="/w/Culinaromancer" title="Culinaromancer">Culinaromancer</a></figcaption></figure>\n<p>A large number of <a href="/w/Quests" title="Quests">quests</a> involve and/or conclude with a battle against a powerful <a href="/w/Monster" title="Monster">monster</a>, which often is or is related to the quest's main antagonist. Except where otherwise noted, these bosses can only be fought in the <a href="/w/Nightmare_Zone" title="Nightmare Zone">Nightmare Zone</a> once their respective quest has been completed.\n</p><p>A sub-boss is a powerful or semi-powerful monster fought as a prelude to the actual boss fight.\n</p>\n<ul><li>The <a href="/w/Abomination" title="Abomination">Abomination</a> is fought during <a href="/w/A_Taste_of_Hope" title="A Taste of Hope">A Taste of Hope</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Agrith_Naar" title="Agrith Naar">Agrith Naar</a>, a <a href="/w/Demon" class="mw-redirect" title="Demon">demon</a> summoned to <a href="/w/Gielinor" title="Gielinor">Gielinor</a> by a group of <a href="/w/Zamorak" title="Zamorak">Zamorakians</a>, is fought at the end of <a href="/w/Shadow_of_the_Storm" title="Shadow of the Storm">Shadow of the Storm</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Ancient_Guardian" title="Ancient Guardian">Ancient Guardian</a> is a golem encountered at the end of <a href="/w/Below_Ice_Mountain" title="Below Ice Mountain">Below Ice Mountain</a>. It is one of the few <a href="/w/Free-to-play" title="Free-to-play">free-to-play</a> bosses.</li>\n<li>The <a href="/w/Arzinian_Avatar" class="mw-redirect" title="Arzinian Avatar">Arzinian Avatar</a> is the boss of <a href="/w/Between_a_Rock..." title="Between a Rock...">Between a Rock...</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Arrg" title="Arrg">Arrg</a> is the strongest <a href="/w/Mountain_troll" title="Mountain troll">mountain troll</a> in the game, and is the boss monster of <a href="/w/Troll_Romance" title="Troll Romance">Troll Romance</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Barrelchest" title="Barrelchest">Barrelchest</a>, a hulking artificial construct controlled by <a href="/w/Mi-Gor" title="Mi-Gor">Mi-Gor</a>, is the boss of <a href="/w/The_Great_Brain_Robbery" title="The Great Brain Robbery">The Great Brain Robbery</a>.</li>\n<li>A <a href="/w/Black_demon_(The_Grand_Tree)" title="Black demon (The Grand Tree)">Black demon</a> controlled by <a href="/w/Glough" title="Glough">Glough</a> is the final challenge in <a href="/w/The_Grand_Tree" title="The Grand Tree">The Grand Tree</a>.</li>\n<li>The <a href="/w/Black_Knight_Titan" title="Black Knight Titan">Black Knight Titan</a> is the scourge of the <a href="/w/Fisher_Realm" title="Fisher Realm">Fisher Realm</a> and is fought during <a href="/w/Holy_Grail" title="Holy Grail">Holy Grail</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Bouncer" title="Bouncer">Bouncer</a> is a powerful <a href="/w/Hellhound" title="Hellhound">hellhound</a>, the pet of <a href="/w/General_Khazard" title="General Khazard">General Khazard</a>, and is fought during <a href="/w/Fight_Arena" title="Fight Arena">Fight Arena</a>.\n<ul><li>Its <a href="/w/Bouncer_(ghost)" title="Bouncer (ghost)">ghost</a> is fought during the <a href="/w/Shadow_Sword_(miniquest)" class="mw-redirect" title="Shadow Sword (miniquest)">Shadow Sword miniquest</a>.</li></ul></li>\n<li><a href="/w/Chronozon" title="Chronozon">Chronozon</a> is a demon who is the boss of <a href="/w/Family_Crest" title="Family Crest">Family Crest</a>.</li>\n<li>A <a href="/w/Corrupt_Lizardman" title="Corrupt Lizardman">Corrupt Lizardman</a> is a <a href="/w/Lizardman" title="Lizardman">lizardman</a> fought during the <a href="/w/Tale_of_the_Righteous" title="Tale of the Righteous">Tale of the Righteous</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Count_Draynor" title="Count Draynor">Count Draynor</a> is a notorious <a href="/w/Vampyre" title="Vampyre">vampyre</a> who is the boss of <a href="/w/Vampyre_Slayer" title="Vampyre Slayer">Vampyre Slayer</a>. He is one of the few <a href="/w/Free-to-play" title="Free-to-play">free-to-play</a> bosses.</li>\n<li>The <a href="/w/Culinaromancer" title="Culinaromancer">Culinaromancer</a> is a powerful sorcerer who draws his power from <a href="/w/Food" title="Food">food</a>. He is the main antagonist of the <a href="/w/Recipe_for_Disaster" title="Recipe for Disaster">Recipe for Disaster</a> quest series, and is the final boss of its conclusion, <a href="/w/Defeating_the_Culinaromancer" class="mw-redirect" title="Defeating the Culinaromancer">Defeating the Culinaromancer</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Cuthbert" title="Cuthbert">Cuthbert, Lord of Dread</a> is a joke boss fought toward the end of <a href="/w/The_Ribbiting_Tale_of_a_Lily_Pad_Labour_Dispute" title="The Ribbiting Tale of a Lily Pad Labour Dispute">The Ribbiting Tale of a Lily Pad Labour Dispute</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Dad" title="Dad">Dad</a> is a <a href="/w/Mountain_troll" title="Mountain troll">mountain troll</a> who is fought during <a href="/w/Troll_Stronghold" title="Troll Stronghold">Troll Stronghold</a>.</li>\n<li>The <a href="/w/Dagannoth_Mother" class="mw-redirect" title="Dagannoth Mother">Dagannoth Mother</a> is the boss of <a href="/w/Horror_from_the_Deep" title="Horror from the Deep">Horror from the Deep</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Delrith" title="Delrith">Delrith</a> is an ancient demon who was summoned to destroy <a href="/w/Varrock" title="Varrock">Varrock</a>; he is the boss of <a href="/w/Demon_Slayer" title="Demon Slayer">Demon Slayer</a>. He is one of the few <a href="/w/Free-to-play" title="Free-to-play">free-to-play</a> bosses.</li>\n<li>The <a href="/w/Dramen_Tree_Spirit" class="mw-redirect" title="Dramen Tree Spirit">Dramen Tree Spirit</a> guards the <a href="/w/Dramen_tree" title="Dramen tree">dramen tree</a> within <a href="/w/Entrana_Dungeon" title="Entrana Dungeon">Entrana Dungeon</a>, and is the boss of <a href="/w/Lost_City" title="Lost City">Lost City</a>. Because of the restrictions on <a href="/w/Entrana" title="Entrana">Entrana</a>, no <a href="/w/Weapons" title="Weapons">weapons</a> or <a href="/w/Armour" title="Armour">armour</a> may be used to fight the tree spirit.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Draugen" class="mw-redirect" title="Draugen">Draugen</a> is a spirit fought as part of <a href="/w/The_Fremennik_Trials" title="The Fremennik Trials">The Fremennik Trials</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Elvarg" title="Elvarg">Elvarg</a> is a <a href="/w/Green_dragon" title="Green dragon">green dragon</a> who has decimated the island of <a href="/w/Crandor" title="Crandor">Crandor</a>, where she roosts. She is the final boss of <a href="/w/Dragon_Slayer_I" title="Dragon Slayer I">Dragon Slayer I</a>, and is one of the few <a href="/w/Free-to-play" title="Free-to-play">free-to-play</a> bosses.</li>\n<li>The <a href="/w/Evil_Chicken_(Recipe_for_Disaster)" title="Evil Chicken (Recipe for Disaster)">Evil Chicken</a> is a boss fought during the <a href="/w/Freeing_Sir_Amik_Varze" class="mw-redirect" title="Freeing Sir Amik Varze">Freeing Sir Amik Varze</a> subquest of <a href="/w/Recipe_for_Disaster" title="Recipe for Disaster">Recipe for Disaster</a>.</li>\n<li>An <a href="/w/Evil_Spirit" class="mw-redirect" title="Evil Spirit">Evil Spirit</a> is the boss monster of <a href="/w/Rum_Deal" title="Rum Deal">Rum Deal</a>.</li>\n<li>The <a href="/w/Fragment_of_Seren" title="Fragment of Seren">Fragment of Seren</a> is the darkness within <a href="/w/Seren" title="Seren">Seren</a> made manifest, who serves as the final boss of <a href="/w/Song_of_the_Elves" title="Song of the Elves">Song of the Elves</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Gadderanks" title="Gadderanks">Gadderanks</a> is a human supporter of the vampyric regime in <a href="/w/Morytania" title="Morytania">Morytania</a>. He is fought during <a href="/w/In_Aid_of_the_Myreque" title="In Aid of the Myreque">In Aid of the Myreque</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Galvek" title="Galvek">Galvek</a> is an extremely powerful <a href="/w/Dragon_(race)" title="Dragon (race)">dragon</a> who serves as the final boss of <a href="/w/Dragon_Slayer_II" title="Dragon Slayer II">Dragon Slayer II</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/General_Khazard" title="General Khazard">General Khazard</a> can be optionally fought during <a href="/w/Fight_Arena" title="Fight Arena">Fight Arena</a>.</li>\n<li>The <a href="/w/Giant_Roc" title="Giant Roc">Giant Roc</a> is a large avian fought atop <a href="/w/Trollheim" title="Trollheim">Trollheim</a> during <a href="/w/My_Arm%27s_Big_Adventure" title="My Arm&#39;s Big Adventure">My Arm's Big Adventure</a>. He has the uncommon ability to knock players around the area with his massive wings.</li>\n<li>A <a href="/w/Giant_scarab" class="mw-redirect" title="Giant scarab">giant scarab</a> is fought at the end of <a href="/w/Contact!" title="Contact!">Contact!</a>.</li>\n<li>The <a href="/w/Giant_Sea_Snake" title="Giant Sea Snake">Giant Sea Snake</a> is the boss of <a href="/w/Royal_Trouble" title="Royal Trouble">Royal Trouble</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Glod" title="Glod">Glod</a> is an enormous <a href="/w/Giant" title="Giant">giant</a> who resides in the cloud world above the magic beanstalk that players plant during <a href="/w/Grim_Tales" title="Grim Tales">Grim Tales</a>; he is the quest's boss. He can disable <a href="/w/Prayers" class="mw-redirect" title="Prayers">prayers</a> and force players towards or away from him.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Glough" title="Glough">Glough</a> is a <a href="/w/Gnome" title="Gnome">gnome</a> who causes trouble in the quest, <a href="/w/Monkey_Madness_II" title="Monkey Madness II">Monkey Madness II</a>. He turns into a giant with three phases and must be defeated by the player.</li>\n<li>The <a href="/w/Ice_Troll_King" title="Ice Troll King">Ice Troll King</a>, leader of the <a href="/w/Ice_trolls" class="mw-redirect" title="Ice trolls">ice trolls</a>, is the boss of <a href="/w/The_Fremennik_Isles" title="The Fremennik Isles">The Fremennik Isles</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Ithoi_the_Navigator" title="Ithoi the Navigator">Ithoi the Navigator</a> is a human that is the boss fought in <a href="/w/The_Corsair_Curse" title="The Corsair Curse">The Corsair Curse</a>. He is of the few bosses that can be fought in free-to-play.</li>\n<li>The <a href="/w/Jungle_demon" class="mw-redirect" title="Jungle demon">Jungle demon</a> is a powerful demon who serves as the final boss of <a href="/w/Monkey_Madness_I" title="Monkey Madness I">Monkey Madness I</a>.</li>\n<li>A <a href="/w/Khazard_Ogre" title="Khazard Ogre">Khazard Ogre</a> is one of the bosses of <a href="/w/Fight_Arena" title="Fight Arena">Fight Arena</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Koschei_the_Deathless" class="mw-redirect" title="Koschei the Deathless">Koschei the Deathless</a> is a <a href="/w/Fremennik" title="Fremennik">Fremennik</a> warrior who cannot be truly killed. He must be defeated in battle three times in a row as part of <a href="/w/The_Fremennik_Trials" title="The Fremennik Trials">The Fremennik Trials</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Me" title="Me">Me</a>, who takes the form of players who fight them, is fought at the end of <a href="/w/Lunar_Diplomacy" title="Lunar Diplomacy">Lunar Diplomacy</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Melzar_the_Mad" title="Melzar the Mad">Melzar the Mad</a> is the keeper of <a href="/w/Melzar%27s_Maze" title="Melzar&#39;s Maze">Melzar's Maze</a>. He is a sub-boss of <a href="/w/Dragon_Slayer_I" title="Dragon Slayer I">Dragon Slayer I</a>. He is one of the few free-to-play bosses.</li>\n<li>A powerful <a href="/w/Moss_Guardian" title="Moss Guardian">Moss Guardian</a> must be fought, without <a href="/w/Weapons" title="Weapons">weapons</a>, <a href="/w/Armour" title="Armour">armour</a>, or <a href="/w/Prayer" title="Prayer">Prayer</a>, to obtain the <a href="/w/Consecration_seed" title="Consecration seed">consecration seed</a> in <a href="/w/Roving_Elves" title="Roving Elves">Roving Elves</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Nezikchened" title="Nezikchened">Nezikchened</a> is a <a href="/w/Black_demon" title="Black demon">black demon</a> who is fought three times during <a href="/w/Legends%27_Quest" title="Legends&#39; Quest">Legends' Quest</a>, including at the quest's climax.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Ranis_Drakan" title="Ranis Drakan">Ranis Drakan</a> is fought during <a href="/w/A_Taste_of_Hope" title="A Taste of Hope">A Taste of Hope</a>.</li>\n<li>The <a href="/w/Sand_Snake" title="Sand Snake">Sand Snake</a>, is the boss of <a href="/w/The_Depths_of_Despair" title="The Depths of Despair">The Depths of Despair</a>.</li>\n<li>The <a href="/w/Sea_Troll_Queen" title="Sea Troll Queen">Sea Troll Queen</a>, ruler of the <a href="/w/Sea_trolls" class="mw-redirect" title="Sea trolls">Sea trolls</a>, is the final boss of <a href="/w/Swan_Song" title="Swan Song">Swan Song</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Sigmund" title="Sigmund">Sigmund</a> is a supporter of <a href="/w/Humans_Against_Monsters" title="Humans Against Monsters">Humans Against Monsters</a> who is fought in two quests: <a href="/w/Death_to_the_Dorgeshuun" title="Death to the Dorgeshuun">Death to the Dorgeshuun</a> and <a href="/w/Another_Slice_of_H.A.M." title="Another Slice of H.A.M.">Another Slice of H.A.M.</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Sir_Leye" title="Sir Leye">Sir Leye</a> is a <a href="/w/Temple_Knight" class="mw-redirect" title="Temple Knight">Temple Knight</a> fought during <a href="/w/Recruitment_Drive" title="Recruitment Drive">Recruitment Drive</a>. He cannot be defeated by any blade; as such, he must be fought either unarmed or with a blunt weapon.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Sir_Mordred" title="Sir Mordred">Sir Mordred</a> is the leader of the <a href="/w/Renegade_Knight" class="mw-redirect" title="Renegade Knight">Renegade Knights</a> and is fought during <a href="/w/Merlin%27s_Crystal" title="Merlin&#39;s Crystal">Merlin's Crystal</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Slagilith" title="Slagilith">Slagilith</a> is an animated golem of rock who is fought during <a href="/w/One_Small_Favour" title="One Small Favour">One Small Favour</a>. It can be fought after the quest is complete.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Slash_Bash" title="Slash Bash">Slash Bash</a> is a strong <a href="/w/Zogre" title="Zogre">zogre</a> who is the boss of <a href="/w/Zogre_Flesh_Eaters" title="Zogre Flesh Eaters">Zogre Flesh Eaters</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Tarn_Razorlor" class="mw-redirect" title="Tarn Razorlor">Tarn Razorlor</a> is a necromancer and is the boss of the <a href="/w/Miniquest" class="mw-redirect" title="Miniquest">miniquest</a>, <a href="/w/The_Lair_of_Tarn_Razorlor" class="mw-redirect" title="The Lair of Tarn Razorlor">The Lair of Tarn Razorlor</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Tolna" title="Tolna">Tolna</a> is a young boy who succumbed to the evils of what later became known as the <a href="/w/Dungeon_of_Tolna" class="mw-redirect" title="Dungeon of Tolna">Dungeon of Tolna</a>. He is the boss of <a href="/w/A_Soul%27s_Bane" title="A Soul&#39;s Bane">A Soul's Bane</a>, taking the form of a three-headed monster.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Treus_Dayth" title="Treus Dayth">Treus Dayth</a>, now a <a href="/w/Ghost" title="Ghost">ghost</a>, was a follower of <a href="/w/Drakan" class="mw-redirect" title="Drakan">Drakan</a> who was sealed within the <a href="/w/Abandoned_Mine" title="Abandoned Mine">Abandoned Mine</a>. He is the boss of <a href="/w/Haunted_Mine" title="Haunted Mine">Haunted Mine</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Ulfric" title="Ulfric">Ulfric</a> is an undead <a href="/w/Fremennik" title="Fremennik">Fremennik</a> who is the boss of <a href="/w/Olaf%27s_Quest" title="Olaf&#39;s Quest">Olaf's Quest</a>.</li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Quests_with_multiple_bosses">Quests with multiple bosses</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/Boss?section=15&amp;veaction=edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Quests with multiple bosses">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Boss?action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section&#039;s source code: Quests with multiple bosses">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Some <a href="/w/Quests" title="Quests">quests</a> have several boss <a href="/w/Monsters" class="mw-redirect" title="Monsters">monsters</a> that must be defeated, usually one after the other.\n</p>\n<ul><li><a href="/w/Dragon_Slayer_I" title="Dragon Slayer I">Dragon Slayer I</a> has two bosses: <a href="/w/Melzar_the_Mad" title="Melzar the Mad">Melzar the Mad</a> and <a href="/w/Elvarg" title="Elvarg">Elvarg</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Spirits_of_the_Elid" title="Spirits of the Elid">Spirits of the Elid</a> has three bosses: The <a href="/w/Black_golem" title="Black golem">black golem</a>, <a href="/w/Grey_golem" title="Grey golem">grey golem</a>, and <a href="/w/White_golem" title="White golem">white golem</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Desert_Treasure_I" title="Desert Treasure I">Desert Treasure I</a> has four <a href="/w/Zamorakian" class="mw-redirect" title="Zamorakian">Zamorakian</a> warriors as bosses: <a href="/w/Dessous" title="Dessous">Dessous</a>, <a href="/w/Kamil" title="Kamil">Kamil</a>, <a href="/w/Fareed" title="Fareed">Fareed</a>, and <a href="/w/Damis" title="Damis">Damis</a>.</li>\n<li>The <a href="/w/Recipe_for_Disaster" title="Recipe for Disaster">Recipe for Disaster</a> quest series culminates in the final subquest, <a href="/w/Recipe_for_Disaster#Culinaromancer" title="Recipe for Disaster">Defeating the Culinaromancer</a>. Six bosses must be defeated: <a href="/w/Agrith_Na-Na" class="mw-redirect" title="Agrith Na-Na">Agrith Na-Na</a>, <a href="/w/Flambeed" title="Flambeed">Flambeed</a>, <a href="/w/Karamel" title="Karamel">Karamel</a>, <a href="/w/Dessourt" title="Dessourt">Dessourt</a>, <a href="/w/Gelatinnoth_Mother" title="Gelatinnoth Mother">Gelatinnoth Mother</a> and the <a href="/w/Culinaromancer" title="Culinaromancer">Culinaromancer</a> himself. Each of these bosses except for the Culinaromancer is a play on another boss of one of the quests required to finish Recipe for Disaster.</li>\n<li>During <a href="/w/Dream_Mentor" title="Dream Mentor">Dream Mentor</a>, four boss monsters are fought, in order: <a href="/w/The_Inadequacy" title="The Inadequacy">The Inadequacy</a>, <a href="/w/The_Everlasting" title="The Everlasting">The Everlasting</a>, <a href="/w/The_Untouchable" title="The Untouchable">The Untouchable</a>, and <a href="/w/The_Illusive" title="The Illusive">The Illusive</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Monkey_Madness_II" title="Monkey Madness II">Monkey Madness II</a> has four bosses: <a href="/w/Kruk" title="Kruk">Kruk</a>, <a href="/w/Kob" title="Kob">Kob</a>, <a href="/w/Keef" title="Keef">Keef</a>, and <a href="/w/Glough" title="Glough">Glough</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Dragon_Slayer_II" title="Dragon Slayer II">Dragon Slayer II</a> has three bosses: <a href="/w/Robert_the_Strong" title="Robert the Strong">Robert the Strong</a>, <a href="/w/Vorkath" title="Vorkath">Vorkath</a>, and <a href="/w/Galvek" title="Galvek">Galvek</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/Song_of_the_Elves" title="Song of the Elves">Song of the Elves</a> has three bosses: <a href="/w/Elven_traitor" class="mw-redirect" title="Elven traitor">Elven traitor</a>, <a href="/w/Essyllt" title="Essyllt">Essyllt</a>, and <a href="/w/Fragment_of_Seren" title="Fragment of Seren">the Dark Lord</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/A_Night_at_the_Theatre" title="A Night at the Theatre">A Night at the Theatre</a> has seven bosses: the <a href="/w/Maiden_of_Sugadinti" class="mw-redirect" title="Maiden of Sugadinti">Maiden of Sugadinti</a>, the <a href="/w/Pestilent_Bloat" title="Pestilent Bloat">Pestilent Bloat</a>, <a href="/w/Nylocas_Vasilias" title="Nylocas Vasilias">Nylocas Vasilias</a>, <a href="/w/Sotetseg" title="Sotetseg">Sotetseg</a>, <a href="/w/Xarpus" title="Xarpus">Xarpus</a>, <a href="/w/Verzik_Vitur" title="Verzik Vitur">Verzik Vitur</a>, and a <a href="/w/Hespori_(A_Night_at_the_Theatre)" title="Hespori (A Night at the Theatre)">Hespori</a></li>\n<li><a href="/w/Desert_Treasure_II_-_The_Fallen_Empire" title="Desert Treasure II - The Fallen Empire">Desert Treasure II - The Fallen Empire</a> has four bosses: <a href="/w/Vardorvis" title="Vardorvis">Vardorvis</a>, <a href="/w/The_Leviathan" title="The Leviathan">The Leviathan</a>, <a href="/w/The_Whisperer" title="The Whisperer">The Whisperer</a>, and <a href="/w/Duke_Sucellus" title="Duke Sucellus">Duke Sucellus</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/While_Guthix_Sleeps" title="While Guthix Sleeps">While Guthix Sleeps</a> has two bosses: <a href="/w/Surok_Magis#While_Guthix_Sleeps" title="Surok Magis">Surok Magis</a> and the <a href="/w/Balance_Elemental" title="Balance Elemental">Balance Elemental</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/The_Heart_of_Darkness" title="The Heart of Darkness">The Heart of Darkness</a> has two bosses: <a href="/w/Prince_Itzla_Arkan" title="Prince Itzla Arkan">Prince Itzla Arkan</a> and <a href="/w/Amoxliatl" title="Amoxliatl">Amoxliatl</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/w/The_Curse_of_Arrav" title="The Curse of Arrav">The Curse of Arrav</a> has two bosses: the <a href="/w/Golem_guard" title="Golem guard">golem guard</a> and <a href="/w/Arrav" title="Arrav">Arrav</a>.</li></ul>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Event_bosses">Event bosses</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/Boss?section=16&amp;veaction=edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Event bosses">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Boss?action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section&#039;s source code: Event bosses">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<p>Some bosses could be fought during <a href="/w/Holiday_event" class="mw-redirect" title="Holiday event">holiday and community events</a> and can no longer be fought.\n</p>\n<table class="wikitable sortable mw-collapsible">\n<tbody><tr>\n<th colspan="2">Boss\n</th>\n<th>Event\n</th></tr>\n<tr>\n<td><a href="/w/King_Snagwort" title="King Easter event</a>\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Boss_slayer">Boss slayer</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/Boss?section=17&amp;veaction=edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Boss slayer">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Boss?action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section&#039;s source code: Boss slayer">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<p>Players who have <a href="/w/Slayer_Rewards#Unlock" title="Slayer Rewards">unlocked</a> the <i>Like a boss</i> ability via spending 200 <a href="/w/Slayer_reward_points" class="mw-redirect" title="Slayer reward points">Slayer reward points</a> can be assigned bosses by <a href="/w/Konar_quo_Maten" title="Konar quo Maten">Konar</a>, <a href="/w/Nieve" title="Nieve">Nieve</a>/<a href="/w/Steve" title="Steve">Steve</a>, <a href="/w/Duradel" title="Duradel">Duradel</a>/<a href="/w/Kuradal" title="Kuradal">Kuradal</a>, or <a href="/w/Krystilia" title="Krystilia">Krystilia</a>. The <a href="/w/Slayer_master" class="mw-redirect" title="Slayer master">Slayer master</a> will randomly assign a boss for which the player meets the below requirements. For example, they can assign the <a href="/w/Dagannoth_Kings" title="Dagannoth Kings">Dagannoth Kings</a> to any player (since there are no special requirements), but <a href="/w/Commander_Zilyana" title="Commander Zilyana">Commander Zilyana</a> can only be assigned if the player has 70 <a href="/w/Agility" title="Agility">Agility</a> and has completed <a href="/w/Death_Plateau" title="Death Plateau">Death Plateau</a>. Krystilia can only assign the bosses located within the <a href="/w/Wilderness" title="Wilderness">Wilderness</a>. These allow players to fight the bosses while enjoying the benefits provided from black masks and slayer helmets, though the player will not be eligible to complete most speed-based <a href="/w/Combat_Achievements" title="Combat Achievements">Combat Achievements</a> while on-task.\n</p><p>After determining the boss, the Slayer Master will ask the player to select the amount that they want to kill for their assignment. The player can select anywhere from 335 kills (36 if <a href="/w/Barrows" title="Barrows">Barrows</a> is assigned). The maximum assignment can be increased by completing <a href="/w/Combat_Achievement" class="mw-redirect" title="Combat Achievement">Combat Achievement</a> tiers, up to a maximum of 65. Upon finishing a boss task, the player will get an additional 5,000 Slayer experience regardless of task length. If the effect of a <a href="/w/Slayer_cape" title="Slayer cape">slayer cape</a> goes off for a boss task, it is possible for the player to be assigned a different boss, since the task itself has numerous options to select from.\n</p><p>If players do not wish to kill the boss they have been assigned, they can pay 30 <a href="/w/Slayer_reward_point" title="Slayer reward point">Slayer reward points</a> to skip the task as with regular tasks. However, this is not recommended, as apart from wasting 30 Slayer points, the task can be easily completed by assigning 3 kills. The only way to "block" a boss is by toggling the ability off, though this <b>does not</b> refund points.\n</p><p><a href="/w/Duradel" title="Duradel">Duradel</a> has a <a href="/w/Slayer_task#Task_weighing" title="Slayer task">task weighting</a> of 12 for boss Slayer tasks, whereas <a href="/w/Konar_quo_Maten" title="Konar quo Maten">Konar</a>, <a href="/w/Nieve" title="Nieve">Nieve</a>/<a href="/w/Steve" title="Steve">Steve</a>, and <a href="/w/Krystilia" title="Krystilia">Krystilia</a> each have a task weighting of 8.\n</p><p>The following bosses can be assigned:\n</p>\n<table class="wikitable sortable lighttable">\n<tbody><tr>\n<th>Boss\n</th>\n<th>Location\n</th>\n<th>Slayer\n</th>\n<th>Other Requirements\n</th></tr>\n<tr>\n<td><a class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/Boss?section=18&amp;veaction=edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Nightmare Zone">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/w/Boss?action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section&#039;s source code: Nightmare Zone">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<p>The <a href="/w/Nightmare_Zone" title="Nightmare Zone">Nightmare Zone</a> is a <a href="/w/Minigame" class="mw-redirect" title="Minigame">minigame</a> that allows players to fight bosses from <a href="/w/Quests" title="Quests">quests</a> they have completed. Players can fight <a href="/w/Nightmare_Zone#Bosses" title="Nightmare Zone">up to 42 unique boss monsters</a> from previous quests.\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">See
